<script type="text/javascript">
						var toggleNav = {
							time : 300,
							state : 0,
							getContDiv : function(obj){
							var tempId = obj.id;
							var contId = tempId.replace(new RegExp('tab','gi'),'blk');
							var contDiv = document.getElementById(contId);
							return contDiv;
							},
							open : function(obj){
							var that = this;
							var cDiv =  this.getContDiv(obj);
							clearTimeout(this._t);
							if(this.preObj ==cDiv){return};
							var t = this.preObj?0:this.time;
							this._t = setTimeout(function(){
								cDiv.style.display = '';
								if(that.preObj){
								that.preObj.style.display = 'none';
								}
								that.preObj = cDiv;
							},t);
							},
							close : function(obj){
							var that = this;
							var cDiv =  this.getContDiv(obj);
							clearTimeout(this._t);
							that._t = setTimeout(function(){
								cDiv.style.display = 'none';
								if(that.preObj){
								that.preObj.style.display = 'none';
								}
								that.preObj = null;
							},this.time);
							}
						};
					</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
			function onLogout(logoutStatus) {
				if (logoutStatus.result === true) {
				jQuery(".blk02_1").show();
				jQuery(".blk02_2").hide();
				jQuery(".blk02_3").hide();
				}
			}

			function onLogin(loginStatus) {
				if (loginStatus.result === true) {
				jQuery(".welcome").html("ćŹ˘čż&#x17D;ä˝ ďź&OElig;"+loginStatus.userinfo.displayname);
				jQuery(".blk02_1").hide();
				if (loginStatus.userinfo.author === 0) {
					jQuery(".blk02_2").show();
				} else {
					jQuery(".blk02_3").show();
				}
				}
			}

			function checkState(data) {
				if (data.result === true) {
				//update login content
				onLogin(data);
				} else {
				sinaSSOController.autoLogin(function(){
					jQuery.ajax({
					'url': 'http://vip.book.sina.com.cn/iframe/ajaxloginv2.php?action=autologin',
					'dataType': 'jsonp',
					'jsonp': 'callback',
					'jsonpCallback': 'onLogin',
					'type': 'get',
					'success': function(data) {
					},
					'fail': function(){}
					})
				})
				}
			}

			function showRecentBooks (result) {
				if (result) {
				var h="", list=result.data.data;
				for (var book in list) {
					h += '&lt;li&gt;&lt;a href="http://vip.book.sina.com.cn/book/index_'+list[book].book_id+'.html"&gt;'+list[book].title.substr(0, 10)+'&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;';
				}
				jQuery(".recent_books").html(h);
				}
			}

			jQuery(document).ready(function(){
				jQuery.ajax({
				'url': 'http://vip.book.sina.com.cn/bookcase/ajax/bookcase.php?bagid=recent&page;=1&psize;=15&extra;=0',
				'dataType': 'jsonp',
				'jsonpCallback': 'showRecentBooks',
				'jsonp': 'callback',
				'type': 'get',
				'success': function(result) {
				},
				'fail': function() {
				}
				});

				sinaSSOConfig = new function() {
				this.entry = 'vipbook'; // ć&oelig;Źäş§ĺ&ldquo; ç&scaron;&bdquo;ć &Dagger;čŻ&dagger;
				this.setDomain = true,
				this.customLoginCallBack = function(loginStatus) { 
					//window.location.href="/default/login";
					processing = false;
					if (loginStatus.result === true) {
					jQuery.ajax({
						'url': 'http://vip.book.sina.com.cn/iframe/ajaxloginv2.php',
						'crossDomain': true,
						'dataType': 'jsonp',
						'jsonp': 'callback',
						'jsonpCallback': 'onLogin',
						'type': 'get',
						'success': function(data) {
						},
						'fail': function() {
						}
					});
					} else {
					jQuery("#tip_uname").html(loginStatus.reason);
					}
				};

				this.customLogoutCallBack = function(result) {
					if (result.result === true) {
					jQuery.ajax({
						'url': 'http://vip.book.sina.com.cn/iframe/ajaxloginv2.php?action=logout',
						'dataType': 'jsonp',
						'jsonp': 'callback',
						'jsonpCallback': 'onLogout',
						'success': function(data){
						},
						'fail': function(){
						}
					})
					}
				}
				};
				sinaSSOController = new SSOController();
				sinaSSOController.init();

				var processing = false;
				var login = function(){
				if (!processing) {
					var uname = jQuery("#username").val(), pwd = jQuery("#password").val()
					do {
					if (uname === "") {
						jQuery("#tip_uname").html("čŻˇĺĄŤĺ&dagger;&trade;ç&rdquo;¨ć&circ;ˇĺ??");
						break;
					}
					if (pwd === "") {
						jQuery("#tip_pwd").html("čŻˇĺĄŤĺ&dagger;&trade;ĺŻ&dagger;ç  ");
						break;
					}
					processing = true;
					sinaSSOController.login(uname, pwd);
					} while (0);
				}
				};

				var enterLogin = function(e){
				var code= (e.keyCode ? e.keyCode : e.which);
				if (code == 13) {
					login();
				}
				};

				jQuery("#loginBtn").click(login);

				jQuery(".logout").click(function(){
				setTimeout(sinaSSOController.logout, 0);
				//sinaSSOController.logout();
				});

				jQuery("#username").focus(function(){
				jQuery("#tip_uname").html("");
				jQuery("#tip_pwd").html("");
				}).blur(function(){
				}).keypress(enterLogin);

				jQuery("#password").focus(function(){
				jQuery("#tip_uname").html("");
				jQuery("#tip_pwd").html("");
				}).blur(function(){
				}).keypress(enterLogin);

				jQuery.ajax({
				'url': 'http://vip.book.sina.com.cn/iframe/ajaxloginv2.php?action=checkstate',
				'dataType': 'jsonp',
				'jsonp': 'callback',
				'jsonpCallback': 'checkState',
				'type': 'get',
				'success': function(data){
				},
				'fail': function(){
				}
				});
			});
		</script>

function comments_tab(id) {
	if (!jQuery('#blog_list')){return false;}
	if (id=='0') {
		jQuery('#tab_0').attr('class', 'on');
		jQuery('#tab_1').attr('class', 'off');
		jQuery('#lnk_0').css('display', '');
		jQuery('#lnk_1').css('display', 'none');
		jQuery('#comment_list').css('display', '');
		jQuery('#blog_list').css('display', 'none');
	} else {
		jQuery('#tab_0').attr('class', 'off');
		jQuery('#tab_1').attr('class', 'on');
		jQuery('#lnk_0').css('display', 'none');
		jQuery('#lnk_1').css('display', '');
		jQuery('#comment_list').css('display', 'none');
		jQuery('#blog_list').css('display', '');
	}
}

    &lt;script type="text/javascript"&gt;
    jQuery.cookie = function(name, value, options) {
        if (typeof value != 'undefined') { // name and value given, set cookie
            options = options || jQuery.cookie.options;
            if (value === null) {
                value = '';
                options.expires = -1;
            }
            var expires = '';
            if (options.expires &amp;&amp; (typeof options.expires == 'number' || options.expires.toUTCString)) {
                var date;
                if (typeof options.expires == 'number') {
                    date = new Date();
                    date.setTime(date.getTime() + (options.expires * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
                } else {
                    date = options.expires;
                }
                expires = '; expires=' + date.toUTCString(); // use expires attribute, max-age is not supported by IE
            }
            var path = options.path ? '; path=' + options.path : '';
            var domain = options.domain ? '; domain=' + options.domain : '';
            var secure = options.secure ? '; secure' : '';
            var cookieValue = [name, '=', encodeURIComponent(value), expires, path, domain, secure].join('');
            document.cookie = cookieValue;
            //console.log(cookieValue);
        } else { // only name given, get cookie
            var cookieValue = null;
            if (document.cookie &amp;&amp; document.cookie != '') {
                var cookies = document.cookie.split(';');
                for (var i = 0; i &lt; cookies.length; i++) {
                    var cookie = jQuery.trim(cookies[i]);
                    // Does this cookie string begin with the name we want?
                    if (cookie.substring(0, name.length + 1) == (name + '=')) {
                        cookieValue = decodeURIComponent(cookie.substring(name.length + 1));
                        break;
                    }
                }
            }
            return cookieValue;
        }
    };
    $.cookie.options = { // ÉčÖĂcookie options
            domain: window.location.hostname,
            path: '/'
    }

    function tips_pop() {
        if($.cookie('view')) {
            return false;
        }
        var MsgPop=document.getElementById("winpop");
        var popH=parseInt(MsgPop.style.height);//˝ŤśÔĎóľÄ¸ßśČ×ŞťŻÎŞĘý×Ö
        if (popH==0) {
            MsgPop.style.display="block";//ĎÔĘžŇţ˛ŘľÄ´°żÚ
            show=setInterval("changeH('up')",2);
        }
        else {
            $.cookie('view', 'yes');
            hide=setInterval("changeH('down')",2);
        }
    }
    function changeH(str) {
    var MsgPop=document.getElementById("winpop");
    var popH=parseInt(MsgPop.style.height);
    if(str=="up"){
    if (popH&lt;=210){
    MsgPop.style.height=(popH+4).toString()+"px";
    }
    else{
    clearInterval(show);
    }
    }
    if(str=="down"){
    if (popH&gt;=4){
    MsgPop.style.height=(popH-4).toString()+"px";
    }
    else{
    clearInterval(hide);
    MsgPop.style.display="none";  //Ňţ˛ŘDIV
    }
    }
    }

    document.getElementById('winpop').style.height='0px';
    setTimeout("tips_pop()",800);
    }

	function addEvent(obj,eventType,func){if(obj.attachEvent){obj.attachEvent("on" + eventType,func);}else{obj.addEventListener(eventType,func,false)}};
	function eventhing(){
		var isIE6 = navigator.appVersion.indexOf("MSIE 6")!=-1?true:false;
		var theSTop = 0,theSLeft = 0;
		if(isIE6){
			divObj.style.position = "absolute";
			theSTop = document.documentElement.scrollTop;
			//divObj.style.display='none';
			divObj.style.visibility='visible';
			if(theSTop &gt; 0){		
				//divObj.style.display='';		
			}else{			
				//divObj.style.display='none';			
			};
			divObj.style.bottom = document.documentElement.clientHeight + theSTop + 'px';
		}else{
			divObj.style.position = "fixed";
			theSTop = document.documentElement.scrollTop || document.body.scrollTop; 
			if(theSTop &gt; 0){
				//divObj.style.display='';
			}else{
				//divObj.style.display='none';
			};		

		};
		theSLeft = (document.documentElement.clientWidth - pageWidth) / 2;
			if(theSLeft &lt; 0){
				theSLeft = - document.documentElement.scrollLeft;
			};
		//divObj.style.left = theSLeft + mLeft + "px";	
		divObj.style.right = 0 + 'px';
	}
	addEvent(window,"scroll",eventhing);
	addEvent(window,"resize",eventhing);
	eventhing();
}();
//--&gt;&lt;!]]&gt;
	</script>
